pārāyaṇena vedānāṃ sarveṣāṃ phalamāpyate
tasya puṇyaṃ na jānāmi cintite cā'kṣare pare
kāśyāṃ nityaṃ pravastavyaṃ sevyottaravahā sadā
āpadyapi hi ghorāyāṃ kāśī tyājyā na kutracit
yataḥ sarvāpadāṃ hartā trātā viśvapatiḥ prabhuḥ
avandhyaṃ divasaṃ kuryātsnānadānajapādibhiḥ
yataḥ kāśyāṃ kṛtaṃ karma mahattvāya prakalpate
kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīni kartavyāni prayatnataḥ
kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīni vyāso vakṣyati yāni vai
teṣāṃ svarūpamākhyāhi skandendriyaviśuddhaye
kathayāmi mahābuddhe kṛcchrādīni tavā'grataḥ
yāni kṛtvā'tra manujo dehaśuddhiṃ labhetparām
atha kṛcchracāndrāyaṇakaraṇādyanantaraṃ na bādhante tatkartṛnnarānityarthaḥ
upavāsena caikena pādakṛcchraḥ prakīrtitaḥ
pratyekaṃ pratyahaṃ pītaṃ parṇakṛcchraḥ prakīrtitaḥ
piṇyākaghṛtatakrāmbuṃsaktūnāṃ prativāsaram
ekaikamupavāsaśca kṛcchraḥ saumyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
haviṣā prātaraśnīta haviṣā sāyameva ca
haviṣā yācitaṃ trīṃstu sopavāsastryahaṃ vaset
ekaikaṃ grāsamaśnīyādahāni trīṇi pūrvavat
kṛcchrātikṛcchraṃ payasā divasānekaviṃśatiḥ
dvādaśāhopavāsena parākaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
ekabhaktenetyādīnāṃ padyānāmityādi satpravṛttiśceti sārdhasaptaviṃśatitamaśloke
nā'nvayaḥ
rājīvaṃ padmam piṇyākaṃ tilapiṣṭaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ ca taṃkraṃ cāmbu ca saktuśca
teṣāṃ pratyekābhyavaharaṇamiti śeṣaḥ
pūrvavat prātarādivat
tryahaṃ prātastryahaṃ sāyaṃ tryahamadyādayācitam
gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ kṣīraṃ daghi sarpiḥ kuśodakam
ekarātropavāsaśca kṛcchraḥ sāntapanaḥ smṛtaḥ
pṛthaksāntapanadravyaiḥ ṣaḍahaḥ sopavāsakaḥ
saptāhena tu kṛcchro'yaṃ mahāsāntapanaḥ smṛtaḥ
taptakṛcchraṃ caran vipro jalakṣīraghṛtānilān
etāṃstryahaṃ pibeduṣṇān sakṛtsnāyī samāhitaḥ
tryahamuṣṇāḥ pibedāpastryahamuṣṇaṃ payaḥ pibet
tryahamuṣṇaṃ ghṛtaṃ prāśya vāyubhakṣo dinatrayam
palamekaṃ payaḥ pītvā sarpiṣaśca paladvayam
gomūtreṇa samāyuktaṃ yāvakaṃ yaḥ prayojayet
kṛcchramekāhnikaṃ proktaṃ śarīrasya viśodhanam
gomūtramityādīnāmekīkṛtya bhakṣaṇam ṣaḍahaḥ ṣaḍahāni
hastāvuttānataḥ kṛtvā divasaṃ mārutāśanaḥ
ekaikaṃ hāsayed grāsaṃ kṛṣṇe śukle ca vardhayet
upaspṛśaṃstriṣavaṇametaccāndrāyaṇaṃ smṛtam
ekaikaṃ vardhayed grāsaṃ śukle kṛṣṇe ca hrāsayet
bhuñjīta darśe no kiñcideṣa cāndrāyaṇo vidhiḥ
caturaḥ prātaraśnīyāt piṇḍān vipraḥ samāhitaḥ
caturo'stamite sūrye śiśucāndrāyaṇaṃ smṛtam
aṣṭāvaṣṭau samaśnīyāt piṇḍān madhyaṃdine sthite
niyatātmā haviṣyasya yaticāndrāyaṇaṃ smṛtam
yathākathañcitpiṇḍānāṃ tisro'śītīḥ samāhitaḥ
vidyātapobhyāṃ bhūtātmā buddhirjñānena śuddhyati
vyuṣṭaḥ prāptaprātaḥ kālaḥ
śiśucāndrāyaṇaṃ brahmacāricāndrāyaṇam
tacca jñānaṃ bhavetpuṃsāṃ samyakkāśīniṣevaṇāt
kāśīniṣevaṇena syādviśveśakaruṇodayaḥ
tato mahodayāvāptiḥ karmanirmūlanakṣamā
ataḥ kāśyāṃ prayatnena snānaṃ dānaṃ tapo japaḥ
vrataṃ purāṇaśravaṇaṃ smṛtyuktādhyaniṣevaṇam
pratikṣaṇaṃ pratidinaṃ viśveśapadacintanam
liṅgārcanaṃ trikālaṃ ca liṅgasyāpi pratiṣṭhitiḥ
sādhubhiḥ saha saṃlāpo jalpaḥ śiva śiveti ca
atitheścāpi satkāro maitrī tīrthanivāsibhiḥ
āstikyabuddhirvinayo mānāmānasamānadhīḥ
apratigrahavṛttiśca matiścānugrahātmikā
ityādisatpravṛttiśca kartavyā kṣetravāsinā
nityaṃ triṣavaṇasnāyī nityaṃ bhikṣākṛtāśanaḥ
liṅgapūjārcako nityamitthaṃ vyāso vasetpurā
ekadā tasya jijñāsāṃ kartuṃ devīṃ haro'vadat
adya bhikṣāṭanaṃ prāpte vyāse paramadhārmike
tathetyuktvā bhavānī sā bhavaṃ bhavanivāraṇam
namaskṛtya pratigṛhaṃ tasya bhikṣāṃ nyaṣedhayat
sa muniḥ sahitaḥ śiṣyairbhikṣāmaprāpya dūnavat
velātikramamālokya punarbabhrāma tāṃ purīm
gṛhe gṛhe pariprāptā bhikṣānyaiḥ sarvabhikṣukaiḥ
tadahninā'labhad bhikṣāṃ saśiṣyaḥ sa muniḥ kvacit
atha sāyantanaṃ karma kṛtvā chātraiḥ samanvitaḥ
upoṣaṇaparo bhūtvā tathaivāsīdaharniśam
athā'nyedyurmunirvyāsaḥ kṛtvā mādhyāhnikaṃ vidhim
yayau bhikṣāṭanaṃ kartuṃ saśiṣyaḥ paritaḥ purīm
bhikṣāṭanaṃ prāpte bhikṣituṃ gate satītyarthaḥ
chatramiva guruṃ gopāyantīti chātrāḥ śiṣyāstaiḥ
ṣaṇṇavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
na kvāpi labdhavān bhikṣāṃ bhāgyahīno dhanaṃ yathā
dvitrāḥ pavitracaraṇāt prāpyā'nujñāṃ guroratha
samācakhyuḥ samāgamya dṛṣṭvardhiṃ tatpuraukasām
śiṣyā ūcuḥ
śṛṇvantvārādhyacaraṇā nopasargo'tra kaścana
nānnakṣayo vā sarvasyāṃ nagaryāmiha kutracit
yatra viśveśvaraḥ sākṣādyatrā'maradhunī svayam
tyādṛśā yatra munayaḥ kva bhīstatropasargajā
samṛddhiryā gṛhasthānāmiha viśveśituḥ puri
yāvanti santi viśveśanirmālyopabhujāṃ gṛhe
pavitracaraṇādārādhyacaraṇāt
viśveśanirmālyopabhujāṃ laiṅgikānāṃ devalakānāmiti vā
gṛhe gṛhe'tra dhānyānāṃ rāśayo yādṛśaḥ punaḥ
na tādṛśaḥ kalpavṛkṣadattā aindre pure kvacit
yatra sākṣād viśālākṣī suvistāraphalapradā
nirvāṇalakṣmyāḥ sadane tyasminnānandakānane
sīmantinyaḥ striyaḥ sarvāḥ pativrataparāyaṇāḥ
sarvā bhavānīrūpiṇyo viśveśārpitasatkriyāḥ
yāvantaḥ puruṣāḥ kāśyāṃ sarva eva gaṇādhipāḥ
sarva eva kumārā vai sarve tārakadṛṣṭayaḥ
tripuṇḍrāṅkitabhālā ye te sarve candramaulayaḥ
upasargasahasraiśca pīḍyamānā apīha ye
na tyajanti sadā kāśīṃ sarvajñā eva te'khilāḥ
gṛhe gṛhe'pi baṭavo brahmavādavivādinaḥ
yādṛśastādṛśa iti ca bahuvacanam
svardhunīdhūtakaluṣāḥ santīha caturānanāḥ
nirvāṇalakṣmīpatayaḥ kṣetrasaṃnyāsakāriṇaḥ
sarva eva hṛṣīkeśāḥ sarve vai puruṣottamāḥ
acyutā eva vijñeyā etatkṣetraparigrahāḥ
striyo vā puruṣā vā'pi sarva eva na saṃśayaḥ
śrīkaṇṭhāḥ sarva evā'tra sarve mṛtyuñjayā dhruvam
mokṣaśrīśritavarṣmāṇastvardhanārīśvarā yataḥ
dharmarāśiḥ paraśvā'tra mahānto'trārtharāśayaḥ
na garbhavāsasaṃsargaḥ kāśīsaṃsthitikāriṇām
enāṃsi nā'tra bādhante viśveśaśaraṇārthinaḥ
yatra viśveśvaraḥ sākṣānnādabindukalātmakaḥ
sarasvatī saridrūpā hyataḥ śāstraniketanam
ānandakānanaṃ sarvaṃ dharmaśāstrakṛtālayam
yāvanto divi vai devāstāvanto'tra mṛṣā na hi
nīrājayanti viśveśaṃ rātrau rātrau sadā'hayaḥ
svaphaṇāmaṇidīpaiśca prāpya kāśīṃ rasātalāt
samudrāḥ sarva evā'tra kāmadhenuvrajānvitāḥ
pañcapīyūṣadhārābhirviśveśaṃ snapayanti hi
mandāraḥ pārijātaśca santāno haricandanaḥ
nīrājayanti nīrājanāṃ prāpayanti
pañcapīyūṣadhārābhiḥ pañcāmṛtasampātaiḥ
yoginaḥ sarva sarva evā'tra kāśīnāthamupāsate
vidyānāṃ sadanaṃ kāśī lakṣmyāḥ kāśī parālayaḥ
muktikṣetramidaṃ kāśī kāśī sarvā trayīmayī
iti śrutvā munivaraḥ pārāśaryo mahātapāḥ
evaṃ babhāṣe tān śiṣyān punaḥ ślokaṃ paṭhantvamum
śiṣyā ūcuḥ
vidyānāṃ cāśrayaḥ kāśī kāśī lakṣyāḥ parālayaḥ
muktikṣetramidaṃ kāśī kāśī sarvā trayīmayī
niśamyeti tadā vyāsaḥ krodhāndhīkṛtalocanaḥ
kṣutkṛśānujcalanmūrtiḥ kāśīṃ śapsyati kumbhaja
vyāsa uvāca
mā bhūtnaipūruṣī vidyā mā bhūtyaipūruṣaṃ dhanam
mā bhūttraipūruṣī muktiḥ kāśīṃ vyāsaḥ śapanniti
iti kṛtvā matiṃ vyāsaḥ kāśyāṃ śāpamadāttadā
datvā'pi śāpaṃ sa munirbhikṣituṃ krodhavān yayau
babhrāma nagarīṃ sarvāṃ kvā'pi bhaikṣaṃ na labdhavān
aṃśumālinamāvīkṣya manāglohitamaṇḍalam
bhikṣāpātraṃ parikṣipya niryayāvāśramaṃ prati
atha gacchan mahādevyā gṛhadvāri niṣaṇṇayā
prākṛtastrīsvarūpiṇyā bhikṣāyai prārthito'tithiḥ
gṛhiṇyuvāca
bhagavan bhikṣukāstāvadadya dṛṣṭā na kutracit
etādṛśaśāpe kāraṇamāha garvaḥ paro'tra vidyānāmiti paro hyatra vidyeti pāṭhe
niṣevate'ghaṃ sa paraṃ sahitaḥ svapitāmahaiḥ
iti śrutvā gatā'marṣo vyāsastāmāha vismitaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
kalā sudhākarasyā'tha kuhūrāhubhayārditā
sīmantinīsvarūpeṇa tiṣṭheḥ kāśyāmanirbhayā
niśi saṅkocinaṃ kāśyāṃ vikāśinyāṃ vaseḥ sadā
kiṃ vā nu karuṇāmūrtiriha kāśinivāsinām
sarvaduḥkhaughahariṇī parā''nandapradāyinī
vārāṇasyāḥ kimathavā'dhiṣṭhātrī devatā tvamu
kiṃ vā nirvāṇalakṣmīstvaṃ yā kāśyāṃ parigīyate
śvapākaṃ yāyajūkaṃ vā prānte'laṅkurvatī samam
madbhāgyaṃ vā pariṇatametadyoṣitsvarūpataḥ
athavā sā bhavennūnaṃ yā kṣetre parigīyate
bhaktapotapradā bhaktyā bhavānī bhavanāśinī
sarvathaiva na nārī tvaṃ nā'surī naiva kinnarī
vidyādharī na no nāgī no gandharvī na yakṣiṇī
tvamiṣṭadevataivā'si kācinme mohahāriṇī
avaśyameva kartā'smi tavādeśyaṃ tadādiśa
ekaṃ tapovyayaṃ hitvā kārayiṣyasi yatpunaḥ
tadevā'haṃ kariṣyāmi vidheyaḥ śubhalocane
na vacastvādṛśīnāṃ hi mahattvaṃ hāpayetsatām
paraṃ tvaṃ kā'si subhage satyaṃ brūhi mamā'grataḥ
iti pṛṣṭā''ha muninā sā viśvāyurghaṭodbhava
viśvāyurviśvaikajīvanetyarthaḥ taduktam yā devī sarvabhūteṣu vṛttirūpeṇa
ṣaṇṇavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
nityaṃ vīkṣye carantaṃ tvāṃ bhikṣāṃ śiṣyagaṇairvṛtam
tvameva māṃ no jānīṣe jāne tvāmahameva hi
prāṇanāthasya me tāvadātithyaṃ saphalīkuru
vyāsa uvāca
ekabhikṣāṃ tadā'haṃ tu kariṣye nā'nyathā punaḥ
tapasvyudīritaṃ śrutvā sā provāca vacastataḥ
aviśaṅkaṃ vada mune kaste'sti niyamaḥ sudhīḥ
iti śrutvā prahṛṣṭātmā sa tāmāha tapodhanaḥ
sudhīriti kaṭākṣaḥ
ayutaṃ mama śiṣyā ye taiḥ sapaktimahaṃ vṛṇe
niśamyeti prahṛṣṭāsyā sā provāca muniṃ tataḥ
kiṃ vilambena tadyāhi sarvān śiṣyān samāhvaya
yena tṛptiṃ gamiṣyanti macchiṣyāḥ sarva eva te
vayaṃ na tādṛmahilā bhartṛsandehakārikāḥ
āyāto'rthī yadā gehe siddhaṃ kāryaṃ tadaiva hi
paripūrṇā diśaḥ sarvāḥ paripūrṇā manorathāḥ
paripūrṇaṃ gṛhaṃ sarvaṃ patyuḥ pādaprasādataḥ
yāhi tūrṇaṃ samāyāhi yāvadannārthibhiḥ saha
iti āśu gatvā samāgaccha yāvannāstamito raviḥ
prahṛṣṭastvaritaḥ śiṣyānāhūya sarvataḥ
āgatya tāṃ punaḥ prāha dṛṣṭvā tanmārgalocanām
mātaḥ sarve samāyātāstvaritaṃ dehi bhojanam
astācalaṃ hi samayā samiyādeṣa bhāskaraḥ
tanmaṇḍapamaṇijyotistatyāhitadinaśriyaḥ
katicitpariviṣṭānnā bhoktumevopaveśitāḥ
tanmārgalocanāṃ vyāsāgamavartmadṛṣṭim
samayā samīpe
jyotistatyā jyotiṣo vistāreṇāhitā samarpitā dinaśrīryeṣāṃ te svarjita
svargamāśriyamiti pāṭhe saudhamadhyaviśeṣaṇam
katicitpariviṣṭānnāḥ katicidbhirjanaiḥ pariviṣṭamannaṃ yebhyaste yathā
taddivyapākasambhārān dṛṣṭvā taddṛṣṭayaḥ kṣaṇāt
parāṃ tṛptimupāgacchan ghrāṇanyāmodarājibhiḥ
atitṛptiṃ samāpannāste tadannaniṣevaṇāt
ācāntāścandanaiḥ sragbhirambaraiḥ paribhūṣitāḥ
atha sāndhyaṃ vidhiṃ kṛtvā propaviśya tadagrataḥ
tāvad vṛddhagṛhasthena gṛhiṇī sā kaṭākṣitā
vyāsa uvāca
svacchāntaḥkaraṇe mātarmahāmiṣṭānnamānade
tvameva dharmaṃ jānāsi patiśuśrūṣaṇe ratā
yadi pṛcchasi māṃ satyaṃ tadā kiñcana vacmi te
vaktavyameva pṛṣṭena manāgapi vijānatā
yenaiṣa toṣamāyāti tava bhartā cirantanaḥ
gṛhiṇyuvāca
sādhāraṇāni dharmāṇi sampṛcche tāni me vada
vyāsa uvāca
anudvegakaraṃ vākyaṃ parotkarṣasahiṣṇutā
miṣṭhānnaṃ ca mānaśceti dvandvaḥ
gṛhastha uvāca
taddāntatā tavaivaikṣi dānaṃ śāpasya cottamam
tvayyeva samyag dṛśyeta parotkarṣasahiṣṇutā
vicārya kāritāyāśca tvameva nilayo mahān
mamaikaṃ brūhi bho vidvan śāpaṃ dadyācca yaḥ krudhā
vyāsa uvāca
gṛhastha uvāca
bhavatā bhramatā vipra nāptā bhikṣā yadāpyaho
tadāparāddhaṃ kimiha varākaiḥ kṣetravāsibhiḥ
tapasvin śṛṇu me vākyaṃ rājadhānyāṃ mameha yaḥ
ṛddhiṃ draṣṭuṃ na śaknoti pariśaptaḥ sa eva hi
tvadvidhānāṃ na yogyaṃ me kṣetraṃ mokṣaikasādhanam
atrā'lpamapi yaddaṣṭyaṃ kṛtaṃ matkṣetravāsinām
taddauṣṭyasya parīpāko rudrapaiśācyameva hi
tacchrutvā vepamānaḥ sa pariśuṣkauṣṭhatālukaḥ
jagāma śaraṇaṃ gaurīṃ luṭhaṃstaccaraṇā'grataḥ
uvāca ca vaco mātastrāhi trāhi bhṛśaṃ rudn
anāthastvatsanātho'haṃ bāliśastava bālakaḥ
śaraṇāgataṃ ca saṃtrāhi rakṣa māṃ śaraṇāgatam
bahūnāmāgasāṃ gehamasmākaṃ duṣṭamānasam
śambhuśāpo'nyathā kartuṃ bhavatyā'pi na śakyate
ahaṃ ca śaraṇāyātastadekaṃ kriyatāṃ śive
pratyaṣṭami sadā kṣetre pratibhūtaṃ ca pārvati
diśa praveśanā''deśaṃ neśastvadvākyalaṅghakaḥ
ityuktā tena muninā bhavānī karuṇājaniḥ
mukhaṃ maheśiturvīkṣya tathetyāha tadājñayā
vyāso'pi niryayau kṣetrāt svāparādhavaśaṃvadan
ahorātraṃ sa paśyan vai kṣetraṃ dṛṣṭeradūragam
prāpyā'ṣṭamīṃ ca bhūtāṃ ca madhyekṣetraṃ sadā viśet
sthito hyadyāpi paśyet sa kāśīprāsādarājikām
svaścāsau aparādhavaśaśca tamātmānaṃ vadatīti tathā chāndaso lugabhāvaḥ
itthaṃ kumbhaja sa vyāsaḥ kṣetre śāpaṃ pradāsyati
kṣetraśāpapradānācca bahiryāsyati tatkṣaṇāt
ata evāvimuktasya kṣetrasya śubhaśaṃsinaḥ
śrutvā'dhyāyamimaṃ puṇyaṃ vyāsaśāpavimokṣaṇam
iti śrīskandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe vyāsaśāpavimokṣaṇaṃ nāma ṣaṇṇavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
iti śrīrāmānandakṛtāyāṃ kāśīkhaṇḍaṭīkāyāṃ ṣaṇṇavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
etad bhaviṣyaṃ śrutvā'haṃ vyāsasya śivanandana
āścaryabhājanaṃ jātastīrthāni kathayā'dhunā
ānandakānane yāni yatra santi ṣaḍānana
tāni liṅgasvarūpāṇi samācakṣva mamā'grataḥ
yādṛśaḥ kathito vacmi tādṛśaṃ śṛṇu kumbhaja
tāni tānīha me kāśyāṃ tatra tatra vada prabho
śṛṇu devi viśālākṣi tīrthaṃ liṅgamudāhṛtam
jalāśaye'pi tīrthākhyā jātā mūrtiparigrahāt
kṣetratīrthānāṃ kriyate sarvapāpanut
he viśālākṣi tarhi jalāśayādeḥ kathaṃ tīrthatvaṃ tatrāha jalāśaya iti
mūrtayo brahmaviṣṇvarkaśivavighneśvarādikāḥ
vārāṇasyāṃ mahādevaḥ prathamaṃ tīrthamucyate
kṣetrapūrvottare bhāge taddṛṣṭaṃ paśupāśahṛt
tatpaścādvigrahavatī pūjyā vārāṇasī naraiḥ
mahādevasya pūrveṇa goprekṣaṃ liṅgamuttamam
golokātpreṣitā gāvaḥ pūrvaṃ yacchambhunā svayam
mūrtirūpaṃ liṅgamityanvayaḥ
paśavo jīvāsteṣāṃ pāśāścaturviṃśatitattvāni taddhṛt
vārāṇasīṃ samāyātā goprekṣaṃ tattataḥ smṛtam
goprekṣāddakṣiṇe bhāge dadhīcīśvarasaṃjñitam
taddarśanād bhavetpuṃsāṃ phalaṃ yajñasamudbhavam
atrīśvaraṃ tu tavyācyāṃ madhukaiṭabhapūjitam
liṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvā prayatnena vaiṣṇavaṃ padamṛcchati
goprekṣātpūrvadigbhāge liṅgaṃ vai vijcaraṃ smṛtam
tasya sampūjanānmartyo vijvaro jāyate kṣaṇāt
vedeśvarādudīcyāṃ tu kṣetrajñaścādikeśavaḥ
dṛṣṭaṃ tribhuvanaṃ sarvaṃ tasya sandarśanāddhruvam
saṅgameśvaramālokya tavyācyāṃ jāyate'naghaḥ
tatra śāntikarī gaurī pūjitā śāntikṛd bhavet
kṣetrajña īśvaraḥ
vidhinā sthāpitamiti śeṣaḥ
varaṇāyāstaṭe pūrve pūjyaṃ kuntīśvaraṃ nṛbhiḥ
tatpūjanāt prajāyante putrā nijakulojjcalāḥ
kuntīśvarāduttaratastīrthaṃ vai kāpilo hṛdaḥ
tatra vai snānamātreṇa vṛṣabhadhvajapūjanāt
tatra śrāddhe kṛte putraiḥ pitṛlokaṃ prayānti te
ānusūyeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ goprekṣāduttare mune
taddarśanād bhavetstrīṇāṃ pātivratyaphalaṃ sphuṭam
talliṅgapūrvadigbhāge pūjyaḥ siddhivināyakaḥ
yāṃ siddhiṃ yaḥ samīheta sa tāmāpnoti tannateḥ
hiraṇyakaśiporliṅgaṃ gaṇeśātpaścime tataḥ
kuntīśvaraṃ pṛthayā sthāpitam kumbhīśvaramiti kvacit
rauravādiṣu ādiśabdena mahārauravādayo gṛhyante
yāṃ siddhimabhīṣṭāṃ siddhim tannateḥ tasya namaskārataḥ
hiraṇyakūpastatrā'sti hiraṇyāśvasamṛddhikṛt
muṇḍāsureśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ tatpratīcyāṃ ca siddhidam
abhīṣṭadaṃ tu nairṛtyāṃ goprekṣād vṛṣabheśvaram
mune skandeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ mahādevasya paścime
talliṅgapūjanānnṛṇāṃ bhavenmama salokatā
tatpārśvato hi śākheśo viśākheśaśca tatra vai
teṣāmapi hi liṅgāni tatra santi sahasraśaḥ
taddarśanād bhavetpuṃsāṃ tattadgaṇasalokatā
nandīśvarāṭhātīcyāṃ ca śilādeśaḥ kudhīharaḥ
mahābalapradastatra hiraṇyākṣeśvaraḥ śubhaḥ
taddakṣiṇe'ṭṭahāsākhyaṃ liṅga sarvasukhapradam
taduttare prasannodaṃ kuṇḍaṃ nairmalyadaṃ nṛṇām
pratīcyāmaṭṭahāsasya mitrāvaruṇanāmanī
liṅge tallokade pūjye mahāpātakahāriṇī
naiṛtyāṃ cā'ṭṭahāsasya vṛddhavāsiṣṭhasaṃjñakam
liṅgaṃ tatpūjanātpuṃsāṃ jñānamutpadyate mahat
vasiṣṭheśasamīpasthaḥ kṛṣṇeśo viṣṇulokadaḥ
tadyāmyāṃ yājñavalkyeśo brahmatejovivardhanaḥ
svayaṃ līnaḥ śivo yatra bhaktānugrahakāmyayā
ataḥ svalīnaṃ tatpūrve liṅgaṃ pūjyaṃ prayatnataḥ
sadaiva jñānaniṣṭhānāṃ paramānandamicchatām
yā gatirvihitā teṣāṃ svalīne sā tanutyajām
vairocaneśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ svalīnātpurataḥ sthitam
tatraiva liṅgaṃ bāṇeśaṃ pūjitaṃ sarvakāmadam
candreśvarasya pūrveṇa liṅgaṃ vidyeśvarābhidham
taddakṣiṇe tu vīreśo mahāsiddhividhāyakaḥ
pañcamudraṃ mahāpīṭhaṃ tajjñeyaṃ sarvasiddhidam
tatra japtā mahāmantrāḥ kṣipraṃ siddhyanti nā'nyathā
tatpīṭhe vāyukoṇe tu sampūjyaḥ sagareśvaraḥ
tadīśāne ca vālīśastiryagyoninivārakaḥ
mahāpāpaughavidhvaṃsī sugrīveśastaduttare
āśvineyeśvarau pūjyau gaṅgāyāḥ paścime taṭe
taduttare bhadrahṛdo gavāṃ kṣīreṇa pūritaḥ
pūrvābhādrapadāyuktā paurṇamāsī yadā bhavet
tadā puṇyatamaḥ kālo vājimedhaphalapradaḥ
golokaṃ prāpnuyāttasmātpuṇyānnaivā'tra saṃśayaḥ
bhadreśvarādyātudhānyāmupaśāntaśivo mune
tasya liṅgasya saṃsparśātparāṃ śāntiṃ samṛcchati
upaśāntaśivaṃ liṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvā janmaśatārjitam
tyajedaśreyasorāśiṃ śreyorāśiṃ ca vindati
āśvineyeśvarau aśvinīkumārābhyāṃ sthāpitau
yātudhānyāṃ nairṛtyām
śivalokamavāpnoti bhāvitenāntarātmanā
tannairṛte ca śūleśo draṣṭavyaśca prayatnataḥ
śūlaṃ tatra purā nyastaṃ snānārthaṃ varavarṇini
hṛdastatra samutpannaḥ śūleśasyā'grato mahān
snānaṃ kṛtvā hade tatra dṛṣṭvā śūleśvaraṃ vibhum
liṅgaṃ ca sthāpitaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kuṇḍaṃ cā'pi śubhaṃ kṛtam
tatraṃ kuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā vai nāradeśvaram
saṃsārābdhiṃ mahāghoraṃ santarennā'tra saṃśayaḥ
tadagre tāmrakuṇḍaṃ ca tatra snāto na garbhabhākū
vighnahartā gaṇādhyakṣastadvāyavye gaṇādhyakṣastadvāyavye suvighnahṛt
anārakeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ tadudagdiśi cottamam
kuṇḍaṃ cā'nārakākhyaṃ vai tatra snāto na nārakī
varaṇāyāstaṭe ramye varaṇeśastaduttare
tatra pāśupataḥ siddhastvakṣapādo mahāmune
anenaiva śarīreṇa śāśvatīṃ siddhimāgataḥ
tatpaścime ca śaileśaḥ paranirvāṇakāmadaḥ
koṭīśvaraṃ tu tadyāmyāṃ liṅgaṃ śāśvatasiddhidam
koṭitīrthe hade snātvā koṭīśaṃ paripūjya ca
gavāṃ koṭipradānasya phalamāpnoti mānavaḥ
mahāśmaśānastambho'sti koṭīśād vahnidik sthitaḥ
tatraiva tīrthaṃ paramaṃ kapāleśasamīpataḥ
kapālamocanaṃ nāma tatra snāto'śvamedhabhāk
ṛṇamocanatīrthaṃ tu tadudagdiśi śobhanam
tatraivā'ṅgārakaṃ tīrthaṃ kuṇḍaṃ kuṇḍaṃ cā'ṅgāranirmalam
snātvā'ṅgārakatīrthe tu bhaved bhūyo na garbhabhāk
aṅgāravārayuktāyāṃ caturthyāṃ snāti yo naraḥ
vyādhibhirnā'bhibhūyeta na ca duḥkhī kadācana
viśvakarmeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ jñānadaṃ ca taduttare
mahāmuṇḍeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ tasya dakṣiṇataḥ śubham
śmaśānavadatibhīṣaṇatvāt śmaśānastambhaḥ kulastambha iti prasiddhaḥ
bhavati ca bhavatyeva ṛṇataḥ ṛṇatrayāt aṅgāranirmalaṃ jvaladaṅgāravadujjva
kūpaḥ śubhodanāmā'pi snātavyaṃ tatra niścitam
tatra muṇḍamayī mālā mayā kṣiptā'tiśobhanā
mahāmuṇḍā tato devī samutpannā'ghahāriṇī
khaṭvāṅgaṃ ca dhṛtaṃ tatra khaṭvāṅgeśastato'bhavat
niṣpāpo jāyate martyaḥ khaṭna ṃ śavilokanāt
bhuvaneśastato yāmyāṃ kuṇḍaṃ ca bhuvaneśvaram
tatra kuṇḍe naraḥ snāto bhuvaneśo bhavennaraḥ
tadyāmyāṃ vimaleśaśca kuṇḍaṃ ca vimalodakam
tatra snātvā vilokyeśaṃ vimalo jāyate naraḥ
tatra pāśupataḥ siddhaḥ tryambako nāma nāmataḥ
bhṛgorāyatanaṃ tasya paścime'tīva puṇyadam
śubheśvaraśca tadyāmyāṃ mahāśubhaphalapradaḥ
tatra siddhaḥ pāśupataḥ kapilarṣirmahātapāḥ
oṅkāra eṣa evā'sāvādivarṇamayātmakaḥ
nādeśaḥ paramaṃ brahma nādeśaḥ paramā gatiḥ
nādeśaḥ paramaṃ sthānaṃ duḥkhasaṃsāramocanam
matsyodarī sā kathitā snānaṃ puṇyairavāpyate
matsyodarī yadā gaṅgā paścime kapileśvaram
samāyāti mahādevi tadā yogaḥ sudurlabhaḥ
uddālakeśvaraṃ liṅgamudīcyāṃ kapileśvarāt
paścime tasyāḥ paścime
taduttare bāṣkulīśaṃ liṅgaṃ sarvārthasiddhidam
bāṣkulīśāddakṣiṇato liṅgaṃ vai kaustubheśvaram
śaṅkukarṇeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ kaustubheśvaradakṣiṇe
saṃsevya paramaṃ jñānaṃ labhedadyā'pi sādhakaḥ
aghoreśo guhādvāri kūpastasyottare śubhaḥ
gargeśo damaneśaśca tatra liṅgadvayaṃ śubham
talliṅgayoḥ samarcātaḥ siddhirbhavati vāñchitā
taddakṣiṇe mahākuṇḍaṃ rudrāvāsa iti smṛtam
caturdaśī yadā'parṇe rudranakṣatrasaṃyutā
tadā puṇyatamaḥ kālastasmin kuṇḍe mahāphalaḥ
rudrakuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā rudreśvaraṃ vibhum
tadagre pitṛkūpo'sti pitṝṇāmālayaḥ paraḥ
tatra śrāddhaṃ naraḥ kṛtvā piṇḍān kūpe parikṣipet
ekaviṃśakulopetaḥ śrāddhakṛdrudralokabhāk
tatra vaitaraṇī nāma dīrghikā paścimānanā
bṛhaspatīśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ rudrakuṇḍācca paścime
gurupuṣyasamāyoge dṛṣṭvā divyāṃ labhed giram
rudrāvāsāddakṣiṇataḥ kāmeśaṃ liṅgamuttamam
taddakṣiṇe mahākuṇḍaṃ snānāccintitakāmadam
rudranakṣatram ārdrā
caitraśuklatrayodaśyāṃ tatra yātrā ca kāmadā
nalakūbaraliṅgaṃ ca prācyāṃ kāmeśvarācchubham
tadagre pāvanaḥ kūpo dhanadhānyasamṛddhidaḥ
nalakūbarapūrveṇa sūryācandramaseśvarau
ajñānadhvāntapaṭalīṃ haratastau samarcitau
taddakṣiṇe'dhvakeśaśca dṛṣṭo mohavināśanaḥ
tatraiva maṇḍaleśaśca maṇḍaleśapadapradaḥ
kāmakuṇḍasya pūrveṇa cyavaneśaḥ samṛddhidaḥ
tadyāmyāmāhutīśaśca dṛṣṭo homaphalapradaḥ
tadyāmyāṃ puṇyajanakaṃ liṅgaṃ pañcaśikheśvaram
tasmin hrade naraḥ snātvā kiṃ bhūyaḥ pariśocati
tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca bhavedakṣayapuṇyadam
dīkṣāṃ pāśupatīṃ labdhvā dvādaśābdena yatphalam
tatphalaṃ labhate vipra martyaḥ kuṇḍeśadarśanāt
mārkaṇḍeyahradātpūrvaṃ śāṇḍilyeśaḥ supuṇyadaḥ
tatpaścime ca caṇḍeśaścaṇḍāṃśugrahaṇāghahṛt
dakṣiṇe ca kapāleśāt kuṇḍaṃ śrīkaṇṭhasaṃjñitam
tatra kuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā dātā syācchrīprabhāvataḥ
mahālakṣmīśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ tasya kuṇḍasya sannidhau
mahālakṣmīṃ samabhyarcya snātastatkuṇḍavāriṣu
tadā tenaiva mārgeṇa yānti strībhirvṛtāḥ sukham
caṇḍāṃśugrahaṇā'ghahṛccaṇḍāṃśugrahaṇaṃ yāvadaghaṃ harati tāvadaghahṛt
tatkuṇḍadakṣiṇe bhāge liṅgaṃ brahmapadapradam
gāyatrīśvarasāvitrīśvarau pūjyau prayatnataḥ
tayoḥ pūrveṇa sampūjyaṃ tapaḥ śrīparivardhanam
ugreśvaraṃ mahāliṅgaṃ lakṣmīśāt pūrvadik sthitam
taddakṣiṇe cograkuṇḍaṃ snānāt kanakhalādhikam
karavīreśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ tasya kuṇḍasya paścime
tasya darśanataḥ puṃsāṃ jāyate rogasaṃkṣayaḥ
tadvāyavye marīcīśaṃ kuṇḍaṃ cā'ghaughanāśanam
tatpaścāccaindrakuṇḍaṃ ca liṅgaṃ cendreśvaraṃ mune
pūrveṇa pūrve
kanakhalaṃ haridvāraṃ gayā vāntaratīrthaviśeṣo vā
indreśāddakṣiṇe bhāge bhāge śubhā śubhā karkoṭayāpikā
tatra vāpījale snātvā dṛṣṭvā karkoṭakeśvaram
nāgānāmādhipatyaṃ tu jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
tatpaścāddamicaṇḍeśo brahmahatyāharo haraḥ
taddakṣiṇe mahākuṇḍaṃ rudralokaphalapradam
tatpaścime mahāliṅgamagnīśa iti viśrutam
āgneyaṃ nāma kuṇḍaṃ ca tatpūrve'gnisalokadam
āgneyeśvarataḥ prācyāṃ kuṇḍaṃ taddakṣiṇe śubham
tatra kuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā svarge vasati pūrvajaiḥ
tatprācyāṃ bālacandreśaścandralokagatipradaḥ
parito bālacandreśaṃ gaṇaliṅgānyanekaśaḥ
vilokya tāni liṅgāni gāṇapatyaṃ padaṃ labhet
bālacandrasamīpe tu kūpaḥ pitṛgaṇapriyaḥ
tatra śrāddhapradaḥ snātvā pitṝn saptā'tra tārayet
āgneyeśvarataḥ prācyāṃ kuṇḍamityanuvādaḥ taddakṣiṇe āgneyakuṇḍadakṣiṇe śubhaṃ
kuṇḍamiti śeṣaḥ
tadandhoḥ pūrvato liṅgaṃ puṇyaṃ viśveśvarāhvayam
viśveśvarasya pūrveṇa vṛddhakāleśvaro haraḥ
yaistu tatrodakaṃ pītaṃ strībhiḥ puṃbhiḥ svakarmabhiḥ
tatra kūpe tu yaddattaṃ dānaṃ śivaratātmanām
saṃvarte'pi na tasyā'sti nāśaḥ kalaśasambhava
khaṇḍasphuṭitasaṃskāraṃ tatra kurvanti ye narāḥ
kāleśāddakṣiṇe bhāge mṛttvīśastvapamṛtyuhṛt
liṅgaṃ dakṣeśvarāhvaṃ ca tataḥ kūpādudagdiśi
mahākāleśaliṅgaṃ ca dakṣeśātpūrvato mahat
mahākuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā mahākālaṃ tu yo'rcayet
antakeśvaramālokya tadyāmyāṃ nā'ntakasya bhīḥ
hastipāleśvaraṃ liṅga tasya dakṣiṇato mune
tatrairābatakuṇḍaṃ ca liṅgamairāvateśvaram
taddakṣiṇe śreyase ca liṅgaṃ syānmālatīśvaram
bandīśvaro mahākālakuṇḍāduttarataḥ śubhaḥ
bandikuṇḍaṃ ca vikhyātaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ mahā'ghahṛt
mahākuṇḍe mahākālakuṇḍe
tatra snānena dānena śrāddhenā'kṣayamaśnute
dhanvantarīśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ kuṇḍaṃ tannāma caiva hi
tasya liṅgasya nāmā'nyatkuṇḍanāmā'nyadeva hi
tuṅgeśvaraṃ liṅganāma kuṇḍaṃ vaidyeśvarā'bhidham
sudhāmayyo mahauṣadhyaḥ kṣiptāstatra mahādhiyaḥ
tatkuṇḍasnānatastasmāttalliṅgaparivīkṣaṇāt
naśyanti vyādhayaḥ sarve saha pāpaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ
taduttare halīśeśaḥ sarvavyādhiniṣūdanaḥ
śiveśvaraḥ śivakarastuṅganāmnaśca dakṣiṇe
jamadagnīśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ śiveśāddakṣiṇe śubham
liṅgakuṇḍayoranyanāmanī evāha tuṅgeśvaramiti
sudhāmayyo yā mahauṣadhyo mṛtasañjīvinyādirūpā vartante tā mahāmahauṣadhyastatra
tannairṛtyāṃ ca vyāseśaḥ kūpaśca vimalodakaḥ
vyāsakūpe naraḥ snātvā tarpayitvā surān pitṝn
akṣayaṃ labhate lokaṃ yatra kutrā'bhikāṅkṣitam
vyāsatīrthātpaścimato ghaṇṭākarṇo hado mahān
ghaṇṭākarṇahṛde snātvā vyāseśaparidarśanāt
yatra tatra mṛto vā'pi vārāṇasyāṃ mṛto bhavet
ghaṇṭākarṇasamīpe tu pañcacūḍāpsaraḥ saraḥ
pañcacūḍājale snātvā dṛṣṭvā devaṃ tamīśvaram
svargalokaṃ naro yāti pañcacūḍāpriyo bhavet
gaurīkūpastato'vācyāṃ sarvajāḍyavināśanaḥ
pañcacūḍottare bhāge tīrthaṃ cā'śokasaṃjñitam
mandākinī mahātīrthaṃ tadudīcyāṃ mahā'ghahṛt
tamīśvaraṃ pañcacūḍeśamityarthaḥ
tatra jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā'śokāṣṭamyāṃ madhau naraḥ
muktikṣetrapramāṇaṃ ca krośaṃ krośaṃ ca sarvataḥ
ārabhya liṅgādasmācca puṇyadānmadhyameśvarāt
etadeva sadā prāhuḥ sarve vai prapitāmahāḥ
kaścidasmatkule jāto mandākinyā jalāplutaḥ
bhojayet prayato viprān yatīn pāśupatānapi 尘
mandākinyāṃ naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā vai madhyameśvaram
madhyameśādavācyāṃ ca viśvedeveśvaraḥ śubhaḥ
tadarcanādarcitāḥ syurviśvedevāstrayodaśa
tatpūrve vīrabhadreśoṃ mahāvīrapadapradaḥ
bhadradā bhadrakālī ca tasya dakṣiṇataḥ śubhā
bhadrakālahado nāma tatrā'tīvaśubhapradaḥ
āpastambeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ tatyācyāṃ jñānadaṃ param
hradapaścimato liṅgaṃ śaunakeśaṃ sudhīpradam
hṛde tatra naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā vai śaunakeśvaram
jñānaṃ tatsaṃlabheddivyaṃ yena mṛtyuṃ taratyasau
mataṅgeśasya vāyavye nānāliṅgāni sarvataḥ
brahmarāteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ mataṅgeśācca dakṣiṇe
tatrā''jyapeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ pitṛliṅgānyanekaśaḥ
talliṅgasevayā sarve tuṣyanti prapitāmahāḥ
taddakṣiṇe siddhakūpaḥ siddhāḥ santi sahasraśaḥ
vāyurūpāstu ye siddhā ye siddhā bhānuraśmigāḥ
taiḥ sthāpitaṃ tu yalliṅgaṃ tat siddheśvaramīritam
tasya sandarśanādeva sarvāḥ syuḥ siddhayo'malāḥ
tatpaścime siddhavāpī pītā snātā ca siddhidā
prācyāṃ ca siddhakūpādvai liṅgaṃ vyāghreśvarā'bhidham
talliṅgadarśanānnṛṇāṃ na bhayaṃ vyāghracorajam
jyeṣṭheśvaraṃ ca tadyāmyāṃ jyeṣṭhasthāneti siddhidam
taddakṣiṇe mudāṃ dhāma liṅgaṃ prahasiteśvaram
taduttare nivāseśaḥ kāśīvāsaphalapradaḥ
jyeṣṭhā devī tu tatrā'sti natā jyeṣṭhapadapradā
avācyāṃ vyāghraliṅgācca liṅgaṃ caṇḍīśvarā'bhidham
taduttare daṇḍakhātaṃ saraḥ pitṛmudāvaham
grahaṇā'nantare snānaṃ daṇḍakhāte'tipuṇyadam
jaigīṣavyaguhā tatra tatra liṅgaṃ tadāhvayam
mahāpuṇyapradaṃ liṅga tatpaścāddevaleśvaram
śatakālastatsamīpe śataṃ kālānumāpatiḥ
talliṅgā''virbhave kāśyāṃ kālayāmāsa kumbhaja
talliṅgadarśanādāyuḥ śatavarṣāṇyakhaṇḍitam
śātātapeśastadyāmyāṃ mahājapaphalapradaḥ
taddakṣiṇe kṣapādeśo mahājñānapravartakaḥ
tadagre ca kaṇādeśastatra puṇyodakaḥ prahiḥ
snātvā kāṇādakūpe yaḥ kaṇādeśaṃ samarcayet
tasya dakṣiṇato dṛśyo bhūtīśo bhūtikṛt satām
tatpaścime'ghasaṃhartṛ āṣāḍhīśvarasaṃjñitam
durvāseśaśca tatpūrve sarvakāmasamṛddhikṛt
tadyāmyāṃ bhārabhūteśaḥ pāpabhārā'pahārakaḥ
vyāseśvarasya pūrveṇa dvau śaṃkhalikhiteśvarau
tau dṛśyau yatnataḥ kāśyāṃ mahājñānapravartakau
yatsamāpyā''pyate puṇyaṃ niṣṭhā pāśupatavratam

akṣapādeti cchedaḥ
prahiḥ kūpaḥ

tadīśāne'vadhūteśo
yogajñānapravartakaḥ

taddakṣiṇe gobhileśo mahā'bhilaṣitapradaḥ
jīmūtavāhaneśaśca tatpaścālliṅgamuttamam
mayūkhārkaḥ pañcanade gabhastīśaśca tatra vai
dadhikalpahado nāma tadudīcyāṃ mahāprahiḥ
durlabhaṃ tavyahisnānaṃ durlabhaṃ ca tadīkṣaṇam
narastamāśu saṃvīkṣya kalpaṃ tryakṣapure vaset
gabhastīśāddakṣiṇe tu maṅgalāṃ maṅgalālayām
uddiśya maṅgalāṃ gaurīṃ bhojayedvijadampatī

vadanaprekṣaṇādevī mukhaprekṣeśvarottare

liṅge tvaṣṭrīśavṛtteśau mukhaprekṣottare śubhe

revateśvaraliṅgaṃ ca carcikā'greṇa śāntikṛt

maṅgalodo mahākūpo maṅgalāpaścime śubhaḥ
upamanyormahāliṅgaṃ maṅgalāpaścime śubham

na taddarśanataḥ puṃsāṃ rākṣasānāṃ mahābhayam
taddakṣiṇe varāheśo varāheśo māṇḍavyeśastato yame
taddakṣiṇe pracaṇḍeśo yogeśo dakṣiṇe tataḥ
taddakṣiṇe ca dhāteśaḥ someśaśca tadagrataḥ
tannairṛtyāṃ kanakeśo mahākanakadaḥ satām
taduttare pāṇḍavānāṃ pañcaliṅgāni sanmude
tatpaścāt kalaśeśaśca liṅgaṃ kālā'bhayapradam
citragupteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ tadudīcyāmaghā'paham
citragupteśvarātpaścādyo dṛḍheśo mahāphalaḥ
kalaśeśādavācyāṃ ca graheśo liṅgamuttamam
citragupteśvarāt paścādyadṛccheśo mahāphalaḥ
utathyavāmadeveśaṃ liṅgaṃ yāmyāṃ graheśvarāt
kambalā'śvatareśau ca tasya dakṣiṇataḥ śubhe
tadyāmyāṃ maṇikarṇīśaṃ tadudak paliteśvaram
jarāharaṃ ca tatraiva tatpaścātpāpanāśanam
tadyābhyāṃ nirjareśastannairṛtyāṃ pitāmahaḥ
pitāmahasrotikā ca tatra śrāddhaṃ mahāphalam
tadyāmyāṃ varuṇeśaśca bāṇeśastasya dakṣiṇe
pitāmahamnotikāyāṃ kūśmāṇḍeśastu siddhikṛt
tatpūrvato rākṣaseśo gaṅgeśastasya dakṣiṇe
taduttare nimnageśāḥ santi liṅgānyanekaśaḥ
jarāharaṃ liṅgamiti śeṣaḥ
tatpaścādaditīśaśca cakreśastasya cā'grataḥ
tadagre kālakeśākhyo dṛṣṭapratyayakṛt paraḥ

tadagre tārakeśaśca tadagre svarṇabhāradaḥ

taddakṣiṇe ca rambheśastatraiva ca śaśīśvaraḥ

nāgagandharvayakṣāṇāṃ kinnarā'psarasāmapi

tatpaścime samudreśa īśāneśastaduttare

rāgadveṣavinirmuktāḥ siddhiṃ yānti ca pūjakāḥ
teṣāṃ mokṣo mayā''khyāto na tu te devi mānavāḥ

devasya dakṣiṇe bhāge tatra vāpī śubhodakā

parvaṇi śivarātrau
yaistatra tajjalaṃ pītaṃ kṛtārthāste narottamāḥ
karuṇeśo dayādhāma tadudīcyāṃ samarcayet

viśveśāddakṣiṇe bhāge nikumbheśaḥ prayatnataḥ
kṣetra kṣemakaraḥ pūjyastatpaśvādvighnanāyakaḥ
virūpākṣo nikumbheśādvahnau pūjyaḥ susiddhidaḥ
tadudīcyāṃ mahāliṅgaṃ devayānīśvarā'bhidham

bhavānīśau namasyau ca śukreśātpaścime śubhau

gaṇeśvareśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ sarvasiddhikaraṃ param

talliṅgasparśanādāśu brahmā'pi viśuddhayati
mahāpuṇyapradaṃ cā'nyattatrā'ryaṃ tripurāntakam

tadagre dhruvakuṇḍaṃ ca pitṛprītikaraṃ param

jāto daśarathasyā''sīdrāmo nāma mahātmanaḥ

agre dhruveśāttāreśo vaidyanāthaḥ sa eva hi

tatpurastāddhiraṇyākṣaliṅgaṃ pūjyaṃ hiraṇyadam

taddakṣiṇe vidhīśaśca tadyāmyāṃ vājimedhakaḥ
daśāśvamedhike snātvā dṛṣṭvā talliṅgamuttamam
daśānāmaśvamedhānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ

īpsitaṃ phalamāpnoti mātṝṇāṃ ca prasādataḥ

candrasūryānvayaibhūpaiḥ kedārāddakṣiṇāpathe

karandhameśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ taṭhapratīcyāṃ mahāphalam

janakeśastaṭhapratīcyāṃ śaṅkukarṇastaduttare
mahāsiddhīśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ tatyācyāṃ sarvasiddhidam
siddhakuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā siddheśvaraṃ mahat
sarvāsāmeva siddhīnāṃ pāraṃ gacchati mānavaḥ
śaṅkukarṇeśavāyavye liṅgaṃ vāyavyasaṃjñitam
sarvāśāpūrako'rkavināyaka iti śeṣaḥ
śuṣkayā asīnāmnyā nadyā
tadagre ca vibhāṇḍeśaḥ kaholeśastaduttare

tapasaścā'pi yogasya siddhidā sā'vanī parā
mune śataṃ sahasrāṇi tatra liṅgāni siddhaye
ekā diguttarā devi vārāṇasyāṃ priyā mama
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyaṃ trisatyaṃ nā'nyataḥ priye
uddeśamātraṃ liṅgāni kathitāni mayā mune
dvistriḥkṛtyaḥ sthāpitāni bhaktyā liṅgāni kānicit
etāni yāni liṅgāni yāni kuṇḍāni ye'ndhavaḥ
yā vāpyastāni sarvāṇi śraddheyāni manīṣibhiḥ
eteṣāṃ darśanātsnānātphalamatrottarottaram

sarvaliṅgamayī kāśī sarvatīrthaikajanmabhūḥ
svargāpavargayordātrī dṛṣṭā dehāntasevitā

surā'suroraganarā bhūmibhārāya te'khilāḥ

saṃsārapāragaḥ pūrvastvantyaśvā'ntyajo'pyadhaḥ
sa eva nūnaṃ sarvajñaḥ sa eva hyadhikekṣaṇaḥ
yaḥ pārthivīṃ tanuṃ hitvā kāśyāṃ dhatte sudhāmayīm
śrutvā'dhyāyamidaṃ puṇyaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvatīrtharahasyavat
kāśīdarśanajaṃ puṇyaṃ prāpnoti niyataṃ naraḥ
yaḥ paṭhedimamadhyāyaṃ prātaḥ prātardine dine

sarvaliṅgamayā'dhyāyaṃ yo'muṃ nityaṃ japetsudhīḥ
na taṃ yamo na taṃ dūtā nainamaṃho'pi bādhate

kāśīliṅgāvalīnāmā'dhyāyo japyeta yanmune
agamyāgamanaṃ cā'pi tathā'bhakṣyasya bhakṣaṇam

mahāpāpāni pāpāni jñātā'jñātāni bhūriśaḥ

vilayaṃ yāntyaśeṣāṇi niḥsandehaṃ mamā''jñayā

iti śrīrāmānandakṛtāyāṃ kāśīkhaṇḍaṭīkāyāṃ saptanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
iti yāvatsamākhyāti devo devīpuraḥ kathām
jātā parisamāptiśca mahāprāsādanirmiteḥ
sajjīkṛto rathaścā'yaṃ brahmādyā militāḥ surāḥ
tārkṣyagaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣo dvāri tiṣṭhati sā'nugaḥ
pratīkṣamāṇo'vasaraṃ puraskṛtya munīśvarān

te niśamyā'dya militāḥ prāveśikamahotsavam

divyaṃ rathaṃ samāruhya nirjagāma triviṣṭapāt

athāṣṭanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca

tvānmokṣalakṣmyāḥ sadmani sthātumucitamiti bhāvaḥ

ananyabhāvā api gāḍhamānasā na te punargarbhadaśāmupāsate
kṣaṇaṃ viśantīha nirīhamānasā nirenasaste mama pārṣadā hi
śṛṇvanti puṇyāśca kathāḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthirāste koṭigodānaphalaṃ bhajanti
upendrataptāni tapāṃsi taiściraṃ snātā hi te cākhilatīrthasārthakaiḥ
snātveha ye vai maṇikarṇikāhade samāsate muktijanāśraye kṣaṇam
tīrthāni santīha pade pade hare tulā kva teṣāṃ maṇikarṇikāyāḥ
katīha no santi śubhāśca maṇḍapāḥ paraṃ paro muktiramāśrayo'yam
niścalaśriyi niścalā śrīryasmiṃstasmin
loke khyātirbhavitrīyameṣa kukkuṭamaṇḍapaḥ
bhālanetra samākhyāhi kathaṃ nirvāṇamaṇḍapaḥ
tathā khyātimasau gantā yathā devena bhāṣitam
adāmbhiko'krūramanāḥ sadaivā'tithivallabhaḥ
viṣameṣuśaraistītraiḥ kāritastvapade padam
jahāra kasyacid bhāryāṃ maitrīṃ kṛtvā tu tena vai
agravedī ṝgvedī
vaiṣṇavān dhanino dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇaṃ vaiṣṇavaveṣabhṛt
śaivānnindati mūḍhātmā narakatrāṇakāraṇam
garhayedvaiṣṇavān sarvān śaivaliṅgopajīvikaḥ
iti pākhaṇḍadharmajñaḥ sandhyāsnānaparāṅmukhaḥ
viśālatilakaḥ sragvī śuddhadhautāmbarojjvalaḥ
ahamasmi dhanī ditsurjātyā cāṇḍālasattamaḥ
iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā kaiściccā'ṅgulisaṃjñayā
aṣṭanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
uddiṣṭa upaviṣṭo'sau yo japeddhyānamudrayā
iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā sa gatvā tatsamīpataḥ
daṇḍavāṇipatyā'tha taṃ babhāṣe tadā'ntyajaḥ
kiñcidvastvasti me tattvaṃ gṛhāṇā'nugrahaṃ kuru
athā'kṣamālikāṃ karṇe kṛtvā dhyānaṃ visṛjya ca
kiyaddhanaṃ tavā'stīha papraccha karaṃsaṃjñayā
tacca saṃjñāṃ sa vai buddhvā provācā'tiprahṛṣṭavat
santṛptiryāvatā te syāttāvaddāsyāmi nā'nyathā
na stokamapi dātavyaṃ tadā''dāsyāmi nānyathā
cāṇḍāla uvāca
yāvadasti mayā''nītaṃ viśveśaprītaye vasu
tāvattubhyaṃ pradāsyāmi viśveśastvaṃ yato mama
ye vasantīha viśveśarājadhānyāṃ dvijottama
kṣudrā kṣudrā jantumātrā viśveśāṃśāsta eva hi
paroddharaṇaśīlā ye ye parecchāprapūrakāḥ
paropakṛtiśīlā ye viśveśāṃśāsta eva hi
iti tadvacanaṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā śrutvā prahṛṣṭendriyamānasaḥ
uvāca pārvatīyaṃ taṃ so'grajanmā'ntyajaṃ tadā
ādāsyāmīti cchedaḥ
āyāhi darbhānā''dehi kurutsargaṃ tvarā'nvitaḥ
tatheti sa cakārā''śu pārvatīyo mahāmanāḥ
viśveśaḥ prīyatāṃ ceti procya yāto yathā''gataḥ
cāṇḍālabrāhmaṇaścaiṣa cāṇḍālā''ttadhanastvasau
asāveva hi cāṇḍālaḥ sarvalokabahiṣkṛtaḥ
sa ekadā sampradhārya gṛhiṇyā lokadūṣitaḥ
jagāma kīkaṭān deśāṃstyaktvā vārāṇasīṃ purīm
pārvatīyo yātaḥ svadeśaṃ gataḥ
dhikkṛtaḥ tiraskṛtaḥ
pāde'kṣarādhikyamārṣam
nītvā te tamaraṇyānīṃ taskarāḥ saparicchadam
tvāṃ vayaṃ ghātayiṣyāmo niścitaṃ saparicchadam
aho pratigṛhītaṃ me yadarthaṃ vasu bhūriśaḥ
kuṭumbamapi tannaṣṭaṃ naṣṭaścā'pi pratigrahaḥ
jīvitaṃ cā'pi me naṣṭaṃ naṣṭā kāśīpurīsthitiḥ
kīkaṭān gayāpradeśān
sakāñcanaḥ svarṇavān
yugapatsarvamevā''śu naṣṭaṃ durbuddhiceṣṭayā
na kāśyāṃ maraṇaṃ prāptaṃ tasmādduṣṭapratigrahāt
prānte kuṭumbasmaraṇāttathā kāśīsmṛterapi
sā kukkuṭī sutau tau tu tāmracūḍatvamāpatuḥ
prānte kāśīsmaraṇato jātā jātismṛtiḥ parā
itthaṃ bahutithe kāle gate kārpaṭikottamāḥ
tasminnevā'dhvani prāptāścatvāro yatra kukkuṭāḥ
vārāṇasyāḥ kthāṃ proccaiḥ kurvanto'nyonyameva hi
kāśīkathāṃ samākarṇya tadā te caraṇāyudhāḥ
jātismṛtiprabhāveṇa tatsaṅgena tu nirgatāḥ
taiśca kārpaṭikaśreṣṭhaiḥ pathi dṛṣṭvā kṛpālubhiḥ
tandulādiparikṣepaiḥ prāpitāḥ kṣetramuttamam
te tu kṣetraṃ samāsādya catvāraścaraṇāyudhāḥ
jitāhārān saniyamān kāmakrodhaparāṅmukhān
prahāsān matkathālāpān lobhamohavivarjitān
mannāmoccāraṇaparān matkathārpitasuśrutīn
maddattacittasadvṛttīn dṛṣṭvā kṣetranivāsinaḥ
mānayāmāsuratha tān kukkuṭān sādhuvartmanaḥ
krameṇāhāramākuñcya prāṇāṃstyakṣyanti cā'tra vai
cariṣyantaḥ cariṣyanti paryaṭiṣyantītyarthaḥ jitāhārānityādermānayāmāsuratheti
paśyatāṃ sarvalokānāṃ viṣṇo te madanugrahāt
vimānamadhiruhyā''śu kailāsaṃ prāpya matpadam
paśyatāmiti ślokadvayaṃ vākyam he viṣṇo te catvāraḥ kukkuṭā ityanuṣajjate
vimānamadhiruhya suciraṃ kālaṃ matpadaṃ prāpya bhogān nirviśya bhuktvā'tra kāśyāṃ kailāse
vā jñānino bhūtvā tenaiva śarīreṇeti śeṣaḥ śāśvatīṃ muktiṃ prāpsyantītyanvayaḥ nanu
kāśīmṛtānāṃ kathaṃ vimānamadhiruhya kailāse gamanaṃ bhogo vā tatrāha madanugrahāditi
antakāle kāśīsmaraṇānmattoṣaṇājjāto yo madanugraha ete bhuktimuktī mayā prāpaṇīyā
nirviśya suciraṃ kālaṃ divyān bhogānanuttamān
tato'tra jñānino bhūtvā muktiṃ prāpsyanti śāśvatīm
muktimaṇḍapanāmaitadeṣa kukkuṭamaṇḍapaḥ
caritramapi vai teṣāṃ ye smariṣyanti mānavāḥ
muktimaṇḍapamāsādya śreyaḥ prāpsyanti te'pi hi
iti yāvatkathāṃ śambhurbhaviṣyāmagrato hareḥ
akarottumulo nādo ghaṇṭānāṃ tāvadudgataḥ
provāca nandin vijñāyā''gatya brūhi kuto ravaḥ
namaskṛtya prahṛṣṭā''syaḥ prabaddhakarasampuṭaḥ
tumulo nāda iti liṅgarūpiṇo viśveśasya dhruvaṃ vidāryodbhūto ghaṇṭānāmiva nādo jāta
utthāya devadeveśaḥ saha devyā sumaṅgalaḥ
brahmaṇā hariṇā sārdhaṃ tato'gādraṅgamaṇḍapam
śrutvā'dhyāyamimaṃ puṇyaṃ paramānandakāraṇam
naraḥ parāṃ mudaṃ prāpya kailāsaṃ prāpsyati dhruvam
iti śrīskandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe muktimaṇḍapagamanaṃ nāmā'ṣṭanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
mokṣalakṣmīvilāsaḥ mokṣalakṣmyā vilāsa ullāsaḥ sphūrtismātsa padārthastathā
raṅgamaṇḍapaṃ śṛṅgāramaṇḍapam
iti śrīrāmānandakṛtāyāṃ kāśīkhaṇḍaṭīkāyāmaṣṭanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
śṛṇu sūta yathāproktaṃ kumbhaje śarajanmanā
senānīḥ kathaya tvaṃ me tato nirvāṇamaṇḍapāt
muktimaṇḍapataḥ śambhurbrahmaviṣṇupurogamaḥ
śṛṅgāramaṇḍapaṃ prāpya yaccakāra vadāmi tat
śrīviśveśvaraliṅgasya mahimā paramādbhutaḥ
viśveśasya caritaṃ vaktuṃ prastāvayati śṛṇviti
senānīḥ he kārtikeya
prāṅmukhastūpaviśyeśaḥ sahā'smābhiḥ saheśayā
brahmaṇā'dhiṣṭhitaḥ savye vāmapārśve'tha śārṅgiṇā
vījyamāno mahendreṇa ṛṣibhiḥ parito vṛtaḥ
gaṇaiḥ pṛṣṭhapradeśasthairghoṣaṃ tiṣṭhaddhirādarāt
udāyudhaiḥ sevyamānaścā''vasan mānabhūribhiḥ
brahmaṇe viṣṇave śambhuḥ pāṇimutkṣipya dakṣiṇam
darśayāmāsa deveśo liṅgaṃ paśyata paśyata
ete pāśupatāḥ siddhā ābālabrahmacāriṇaḥ
jitendriyāstaponiṣṭhāḥ pañcārthajñānanirmalāḥ
bhasmakūṭaśayā dāntāḥ suśīlā ūrdhvaretasaḥ
liṅgārcanaratā nityamananyendriyamānasāḥ
sadaiva vāruṇā''gneyasnānadvayasunirmalāḥ
kandamūlaphalāhārāḥ paratattvārpitekṣaṇāḥ
nirīhā niṣprapañcāśca nirātaṅkā nirāmayāḥ
nirbhagā nirupāyāśca niḥsaṅgā nirmalāśayāḥ
nistīrṇodagrasaṃsārā nirvikalpā nirenasaḥ
nirdvandvā niścitārthāśca nirahaṅkāravṛttayaḥ
sadaiva me mahāprītā matputrā matsvarūpiṇaḥ
ete pūjyā namasyāśca mabuddhyā matparāyaṇaiḥ
ete pāśupatā ityādīnāṃ sadaiva me mahāprītā iti ṣaṣṭhenā'nvayaḥ
pañcārthajñānanirmalāḥ pañcānāmakārokāramakāranādabindurūpāṇāmarthajñānena nirmalāḥ
catvāro vedā itihāsapurāṇaṃ ceti vā pañcapañcākṣarīvidyāvarṇānāṃ brahmaviṣṇurudreśvara
sadāśivākhyānāṃ vā'rthajñānānnirmalā iti vā bhasmakūṭaśayā iti bhasmakūṭe bhasma
samūhe śerata iti tathā ca śrutiḥ bhasmacchanno bhasmaśayyāśayāno rudrādhyāyī mucyate
niṣprapañcā dehādyabhimānaśūnyāḥ nirbhagāḥ tyaktaiśvaryāḥ nirdambhā iti
arciteṣveṣyahaṃ prīto bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ
asmin vaiśveśvare kṣetre sambhojyāḥ śivayoginaḥ
ayaṃ viśveśvaraḥ sākṣātsthāvarātmā jagatprabhuḥ
sarveṣāṃ sarvasiddhīnāṃ kartā bhaktijuṣāmiha
ahaṃ kaṃdāciddṛśyaḥ syāmadṛśyaḥ syāṃ kadācana
ānandakānane cā'tra svairaṃ tiṣṭhāmi devatāḥ
anugrahāya sarveṣāṃ bhaktānāmiha sarvadā
sthāsyāmi liṅgarūpeṇa cintitārthaphalapradaḥ
svayambhūnyasvayambhūni yāni yāni liṅgāni sarvataḥ
tāni sarvāṇi cā''yānti draṣṭuṃ liṅgamidaṃ sadā
ahaṃ sarveṣu liṅgeṣu tiṣṭhāmyeva na saṃśayaḥ
parantviyaṃ parā mūrtirmama liṅgasvarūpiṇī
he devatāḥ
iyametatsthānādheyā
yena liṅgamidaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śraddhayā śuddhacakṣuṣā
sākṣātkāreṇa tenā'haṃ dṛṣṭa eva divaukasaḥ
śravaṇādasya liṅgasya pātakaṃ janmasañcitam
kṣaṇātkṣayati śṛṇvantu devā ṛṣigaṇaiḥ saha
avaśyaṃ naśyati kṣipraṃ mama vākyānna saṃśayaḥ
etalliṅgaṃ samuddiśya gṛhānniṣkramaṇakṣaṇāt
rājasūyasahasrasya phalaṃ syātsparśamātrataḥ
pūjāmātraṃ vidhāyā'sya liṅgarājasya bhaktitaḥ
vidhāya mahatīṃ pūjāṃ pañcāmṛtapuraḥsarām
vastrapūtajalairliṅgaṃ snāpayitvā mamā'marāḥ
lakṣā'śvamedhajanitaṃ puṇyamāpnoti sattamaḥ
ghṛtadīpaprabodhaiśca jyotīrūpavimānagaḥ
viśveśe paramānnaṃ yo dadyāt sā''jyaṃ saśarkaram
mukhavāsaṃ tu yo dadyāddarpaṇaṃ cārucāmaram
saṃkhyāsāgararatnānāṃ kathañcitkartumiṣyate
mukhavāsādidānasya kaḥ saṃkhyāmatra kārayet
pūjopakaraṇadravyaṃ yo ghaṇṭāgaḍukādikam
yo gītavādyanṛtyānāmekaṃ maṭhaprītaye vyadhāt
yaḥ sacitrānmahābhogān bhuṅkte matpurataḥ sthitaḥ
sakṛdviśveśvaraṃ natvā madhyejanma sudhīrnaraḥ
yastu viśveśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā hyanyatrā'pi vipadyate
viśveśākhyā tu jihvāgre viśvanāthakathā śrutau
viśveśaśīlanaṃ citte yasya tasya janiḥ kutaḥ
liṅgaṃ me viśvanāthasya dṛṣṭvā yaścā'numodate
same gaṇeṣu gaṇyeta mahāpuṇyabalāśritaḥ
vyadhāt kuryāt
nityaṃ viśveśa viśveśa viśvanātheti yo japet
mamā'pīdaṃ mahāliṅgaṃ sadā pūjyatamaṃ surāḥ
yairna viśveśvaro dṛṣṭo yairna viśveśvaraḥ smṛtaḥ
kṛtāntadūtaiste dṛṣṭāstaiḥ smṛtā garbhavedanā
yairidaṃ praṇataṃ liṃṅgaṃ praṇatāste surā'suraiḥ
dikpālapadataḥ pātaḥ pātaḥ śivanaterna hi
śṛṇvantu devarṣigaṇāḥ samastāstathyaṃ bruve tacca paropakṛtyai
tīrthaṃ kvacidvai maṇikarṇikāsamaṃ liṅgaṃ ca viśveśvaratulyamanyataḥ
smṛtā prāptā
na viśvanāthasya samaṃ hi liṅgaṃ na tīrthamanyanmaṇikarṇikātaḥ
vārāṇasī tīrthamayī samastā yasyāstu nāmā'pi hi tīrthatīrtham
sthānādamuṣmānmama rājasaudhāvyācyāṃ manāgīśasamāśritāyām
savye'pasavye ca karāḥ krameṇa śatatrayī cā'pi śatadvayī ca
hastāḥ śataṃ pañcasurāpagāyāmudīcyavācyormaṇikarṇikeyam
sārastrilokyāḥ parakośabhūmiryaiḥ sevitā te mama hṛcchayā hi
āsaptapātālatalāt svayambhusamutthitaṃ bhaktakṛpāvaśena
ye'smin janāḥ kṛtrimabhāvabuddhyā liṅgaṃ bhajiṣyanti ca hetuvādaiḥ
teṣāṃ hi daṇḍaḥ para eṣa eva na garbhavāsād viramanti te dhruvam
sudhādhāma sudhāmadhāma sudhā'mṛtaṃ kaivalyaṃ tasya dhāma susthāneṣu dvārakādiṣu dhāmnaḥ
svaprakāśasya dhāma sphūrtiryasmāttat yadvā sudhāmadhāma śreṣṭhaṃ sthānamityarthaḥ
mayaiva dattaiḥ śubhavastujātairniḥśreyasaḥ śrīrvasayet satastān
śṛṇuṣva viṣṇo śṛṇu sṛṣṭikartaḥ śṛṇvantu devarṣigaṇāḥ samastāḥ
idaṃ hi liṅgaṃ parasiddhidaṃ satāṃ bhedo manāgatra na matsakāśataḥ
viśveśaliṅgaṃ maṇikarṇikā'mbu kāśīpurī satyamidaṃ trisatyam
utthāya devo'tha saśaktirīśastasmin hi liṅge kṛtacārupūjaḥ
prabhāvasyaikadeśo'yaṃ kathitaḥ kalmaṣāpahaḥ
tavā'gre tu yathābuddhi kāśīviśleṣatāpinaḥ
acireṇaiva kālena kāśīṃ prāpsyasyanuttamām
astācalasya śikharaṃ prāptavāneṣa bhānumān
vyāsa uvāca
rahasyaṃ parivijñāya kṣetrasya śaśimaulinaḥ
kṛtacāru pūjaḥ kṛtā cārvī pūjā yena saḥ saptamyanto vā pāṭhaḥ akhilalokakāmada
iti śrīrāmānandakṛtāyāṃ kāśīkhaṇḍaṭīkāyāmekonaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ
ko'tra varṇayituṃ śaktaḥ sūta varṣaśatairapi
yathā devyai samākhyāyi śivena paramātmanā
tavā'gre ca samākhyātaṃ śukādīnāṃ ca sattama
idānīṃ praṣṭukāmo'si kiṃ tat pṛccha vadāmi te
śrutvā'dhyāyamimaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvakalmaṣanāśanam
iti śrīskandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe viśveśvaraliṅgamahimākhyo
nāmaikonaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ
atha śatatamo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
idaṃ skāndamahaṃ śrutvā kāśīkhaṇḍamanuttamam
nitarāṃ paritṛpto'smi hṛdi cā'pi vidhāritam
anukramaṇikā'dhyāyaṃ tathā māhātmyamuttamam
pārāśarya samācakṣva yathāpūrvamidaṃ bhavet
vyāsa uvāca jātūkarṇya niśāmaya
śukavaiśampāyanādyāḥ śṛṇvantvapi ca bālakāḥ
anukramaṇikā'dhyāyaṃ māhātmyaṃ cāpi khaṇḍajam
pravakṣyāmyaghanāśāya mahāpuṇyapravardhanam
athā'dhyāye śatatame sarvābhīṣṭaphalaprade
pūrvā'dhyāyānte idānīṃ praṣṭukāmo'si kiṃ tat pṛccha vadāmi te ityuktaṃ
tatroktā'nuvādapūrvakaṃ tṛptimāviṣkurvannanukramaṇikātanmāhātmye pṛcchati idaṃ skānda
satyalokaprabhāvaśca dvitīyaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ
agasterāśramapade devānāmāgamastataḥ
tīrthapraśaṃsā ca tataḥ saptaparyastataḥ smṛtāḥ
indrāgnyorlokasamprāptistataśca śivaśarmaṇaḥ
prathamā'dhyāyārthamāha vindhyeti dvitīyā'dhyāyārthamāha satyeti dvitīyo
tṛtīyā'dhyāyārthamāha agasteriti caturthā'dhyāyārthamāha pativrateti
uḍulokakathā tasmāttataḥ śukrasamudbhavaḥ
māheyagurusaurīṇāṃ lokānāṃ varṇanaṃ tataḥ
saptarṣīṇāṃ tato lokā dhruvasya ca tapastataḥ
darśanaṃ satyalokasya tasya vai śivaśarmaṇaḥ
caturbhujā'bhiṣekaśca nirvāṇaṃ śivaśarmaṇaḥ
skandā'gastyośca saṃvādo maṇikarṇyāḥ samudbhavaḥ
tatastu gaṅgāmāhātmyaṃ tato daśaharāstavaḥ
prabhāvaścā'pi gaṅgāyā gaṅgānāmasahasrakam
vārāṇasyāḥ praśaṃsā'tha bhairavā''virbhavastataḥ
pañcadaśā'dhyāyārthamāha uḍḍuloketi tasmāttadanantaramuḍulokakathetyanvayaḥ
śatatamo'dhyāyaḥ
daṇḍapāṇeḥ samudbhūtirjñānavāpyuddhavastataḥ
ākhyānaṃ ca kalāvatyāḥ sadācārastataḥ param
brahmacāriprakaraṇaṃ tataḥ strīlakṣaṇāni ca
kṛtyā'kṛtyaprakaraṇamavimukteśavarṇanam
kālajñānaṃ tataḥ proktaṃ divodāsasya varṇanam
kāśyāśca varṇanaṃ tasmādyoginīvarṇanaṃ tataḥ
lolārkasya samākhyānamuttarārkakathā tataḥ
dvātriṃśadadhyāyārthamāha daṇḍapāṇeriti trayastriṃśadadhyāyārthamāha jñānavāpīti catu
striṃśadadhyāyārthamāha ākhyānaṃ ceti pañcatriṃśadadhyāyārthamāha sadācāra iti
ṣaṭtriṃśadadhyāyārthamāha brahmacārīti saptatriṃśadadhyāyārthamāha tataḥ strīti
aṣṭātriṃśadadhyāyārthamāha kṛtyā'kṛtyeti ekonacatvāriṃśadadhyāyārthamāha avimukte
sāmbādityasya mahimā drupadādityaśaṃsanam
tatastu garuḍākhyānamaruṇārkādayastataḥ
daśāśvamedhikaṃ tīrthaṃ mandarācca gaṇāgamaḥ
piśācamocanākhyānaṃ gaṇeśapreṣaṇaṃ tataḥ
māyāgaṇapateścā'tha duṇḍiprādurbhavastataḥ
viṣṇumāyāprapañco'tha divodāsavisarjanam
tato vaiṣṇavatīrthānāṃ māhātmyaparivarṇanam
prayāṇaṃ mandarātkāśīṃ vṛṣabhadhvajaśūlinaḥ
jaigīṣavyena saṃvādo jyeṣṭhasthāne maheśituḥ
aṣṭacatvāriṃśadadhyāyārthamāha sāmbādityasyeti ekonapañcāśadadhyāyārthamāha
tataḥ kṣetrarahasyasya kathanaṃ pāpanāśanam
tataḥ śaileśvarakathā ratneśasya caṃ darśanam
kṛttivāsaḥ samutpattistataścāyatanāgamaḥ
devatānāmadhiṣṭhānaṃ durgā'suraparākramaḥ
durgāyā vijayaścā'tha tata oṅkāravarṇanam
punaroṅkāramāhātmyaṃ trilocanasamudbhavaḥ
tato dharmeśamahimā tataḥ pakṣikathā śubhā
catuḥṣaṣṭyadhyāyārthamāha tataḥ kṣetreti pañcaṣaṣṭyadhyāyārthamāha athāta iti
athaśabdo'tra liṅgaprādurbhāve maṅgalārthaḥ
ṣaṭṣaṣṭyadhyāyārthamāha tataḥ śaileśvareti saptaṣaṣṭyadhyāyārthamāha ratneśasyeti
aṣṭaṣaṣṭyadhyāyārthamāha kṛttivāsa iti ekonasaptatyadhyāyārthamāha tataścāyata
tato vīreśvarākhyānaṃ vīreśamahimā punaḥ
gaṅgātīrthaiśca saṃyuktā kāmeśamahimā tataḥ
viśvakarmeśamahimā dakṣayajñasamudbhavaḥ
gaṇeśasyā'tha mahimā narmadeśasamudbhavaḥ
satīśvarasamutpattiramṛteśādivarṇanam
kṣetratīrthakadambaṃ ca muktimaṇḍapasaṃkathā
viśveśāvirbhavaścā'tha tato yātrāparikramaḥ
etadākhyānaśatakaṃ krameṇa parikīrtitam
yasya śravaṇamātreṇa sarvakhaṇḍaśruteḥ phalam
anukramaṇikā'dhyāye'pyasti yātrāparikramaḥ
dvyaśītyadhyāyārthamāha tato vīreti tryaśītyadhyāyārthamāha vīreśeti catura
śītyadhyāyārthamāha gaṅgeti pañcāśītyadhyāyārthamāha kāmeśeti
ṣaḍaśītyadhyāyārthamāha viśvakarmeti saptāśītyadhyāyārthamāha dakṣayajñeti
aṣṭāśītyadhyāyārthamāha satyā iti navāśītyadhyāyārthamāha tato dakṣeti
pañcanavatyadhyāyārthamāha vyāsasyeti ṣaṇṇavatyadhyāyārthamāha vyāsaśāpeti
saptanavatyadhyāyārthamāha kṣetreti aṣṭanavatyadhyāyārthamāha muktimaṇḍapeti
sūta uvāca
yātrāparikramaṃ brūhi janānāṃ hitakāmyayā
yathāvat siddhikāmānāṃ satyavatyāḥ sutottama
vyāsa uvāca
niśāmaya mahāprājña lomaharṣaṇa vacmi te
sacailamādau saṃsnāya cakrapuṣkariṇījale
santarpya devān sapitṝn brāhmaṇāṃśca tathā'rthinaḥ
ādityaṃ draupadīṃ viṣṇuṃ daṇḍapāṇiṃ maheśvaram
namaskṛtya tato gaccheddraṣṭuṃ duṇḍivināyakam
navanavatyadhyāyārthamāha viśveśeti śatatamādhyāyārthamāha tato yātreti
jñānavāpīmupaspṛśya nandikeśaṃ tato'rcayet
tārakeśaṃ tato'bhyarcya mahākāleśvaraṃ tataḥ
tataḥ punardaṇḍapāṇimityeṣā pañcatīrthikā
tato vaiśveśvarī yātrā kāryā sarvārthasiddhidā
dvisaptāyatanānāṃ ca kāryā yātrā prayatnataḥ
kṛṣṇāṃ pratipadaṃ prāpya bhūtāvadhi yathāvidhi
tattattīrthakṛtasnānastattalliṅgakṛtārcanaḥ
maunena yātrāṃ kurvāṇaḥ phalaṃ prāpnoti yātrikaḥ
oṅkāraṃ prathamaṃ paśyenmatsyodaryāṃ kṛtodakaḥ
triviṣṭapaṃ mahādevaṃ tato vai kṛttivāsasam
ratneśaṃ cā'tha candreśaṃ kedāraṃ ca tato vrajet
jñānavāpīmiti ślokoktaṃ caturtham
tata iti pādoktaṃ pañcamamityeṣā pañcatīrthiketi pūrvoktarūpā vā
dharmeśvaraṃ ca vīreśaṃ gacchetkāmeśvaraṃ tataḥ
viśvakarmeśvaraṃ cā'tha maṇikarṇīśvaraṃ tataḥ
avimukteśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā tato viśveśamarcayet
eṣā yātrā prayatnena kartavyā kṣetravāsinā
yastu kṣetramuṣitvā tu naitāṃ yātrāṃ samācaret
vighnāstasyopatiṣṭhante kṣetroccāṭanasūcakāḥ
aṣṭāyatanayātrānyā kartavyā vighnaśāntaye
dakṣeśaḥ pārvatīśaśca tathā paśupatīśvaraḥ
gaṅgeśo narmadeśaśca gabhastīśaḥ satīśvaraḥ
aṣṭamastārakeśaśca pratyaṣṭami viśeṣataḥ
dṛśyānyetāni liṅgāni mahāpāpopaśāntaye
aparā'pi śubhā yātrā yogakṣemakarī sadā
śaileśaṃ prathamaṃ vīkṣya varaṇāsnānapūrvakam
snānaṃ tu saṅgame kṛtvā draṣṭavyaḥ saṅgameśvaraḥ
svalīnatīrthe susnātaḥ paśyet svalīnamīśvaram
snātvā mandākinītīrthe draṣṭavyo madhyameśvaraḥ
paśyeddhiraṇyagarbheśaṃ tatra tīrthe kṛtodakaḥ
maṇikarṇya tataḥ snātvā paśyedīśānamīśvaram
kāpileyahade snātvā vīkṣeta vṛṣabhadhvajam
upaśāntaśivaṃ paśyettatkūpavihitodakaḥ
pañcacūḍāhade snātvā jyeṣṭhasthānaṃ tato'rcayet
devasyā'gre tu yā vāpī tatropasparśane kṛte
śukreśvaraṃ tataḥ paśyettatkūpavihitodakaḥ
daṇḍakhāte tataḥ snātvā vyāghreśaṃ pūjayettataḥ
śaunakeśvarakuṇḍe tu snānaṃ kṛtvā tato'rcayet
jambukeśaṃ mahāliṅgaṃ kṛtvā yātrāmimāṃ naraḥ
kvacinna jāyate bhūyaḥ saṃsāre duḥkhasāgare
samārabhya pratipadaṃ yāvatkṛṣṇā caturdaśī
imāṃ yātrāṃ naraḥ kṛtvā na bhūyo'pyabhijāyate
anyā yātrā prakartavyaikādaśāyatanodbhavā
āgnīdhrakuṇḍe susnātaḥ paśyedāgnīdhramīśvaram
urvaśīśaṃ tato gacchettatastu nakulīśvaram
āṣāḍhīśaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā bhārabhūteśvaraṃ tataḥ
lāṅgalīśamathā''lokya tatastu tripurāntakam
tato manaḥprakāmeśaṃ prītikeśamatho vrajet
madālaseśvaraṃ tasmāttilaparṇeśvaraṃ tataḥ
yātraikādaśaliṅgānāmeṣā kāryā prayatnataḥ
imāṃ yātrāṃ prakurvāṇo rudratvaṃ prāpnuyānnaraḥ
aṃtaḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi gaurīyātrāmanuttamān
śuklapakṣe tṛtīyāyāṃ yā yātrā viṣvagṛddhidā
eṣa cāsau kramaśceti etadāyatanāni pūrvoktaśaileśādyāśritāni
viṣvagṛddhidā sarvasampattidātrī
jyeṣṭhāvāpyāṃ naraḥ snātvā jyeṣṭhāṃ gaurīṃ samarcayet
saubhāgyagaurī sampūjyā jñānavāpyāṃ kṛtodakaiḥ
tataḥ śṛṅgāragaurīṃ ca tatraiva ca kṛtodakaḥ
snātvā viśālagaṅgāyāṃ viśālākṣīṃ tato vrajet
snātvā bhavānītīrthe'tha bhavānīṃ paripūjayet
tato gacchenmahālakṣmīṃ sthiralakṣmīsamṛddhaye
imāṃ yātrāṃ naraḥ kṛtvā kṣetre'smin muktijanmani
kuryātpraticaturthīha yātrāṃ vighneśituḥ sadā
brāhmaṇebhyastaduddeśāddeyā vai modakā modakā mude
bhaume bhairavayātrā ca kāryā pātakahāriṇī
ravivāre raveryātrā ṣaṣṭhyāṃ vā ravisaṃyuji
navamyāmathavā'ṣṭamyāṃ caṇḍīyātrā śubhā matā
prātaḥ snānaṃ vidhāyā''dau natvā pañcavināyakān
namaskṛtvā'tha viśveśaṃ sthitvā nirvāṇamaṇḍape
antargṛhasya yātrāṃ vai kariṣye'ghaughaśāntaye
gṛhītvā niyamaṃ ceti gatvā'tha maṇikarṇikām
snātvā maunena cā''gatya maṇikarṇīśamarcayet
kambalāśvatarau natvā vāsukīśaṃ praṇamya ca
parvateśaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā gaṅgākeśavamapyatha
tatastu lalitāṃ dṛṣṭvā jarāsandheśvaraṃ tataḥ
brahmeśvaraṃ tato natvā natvā'gastīśvaraṃ tataḥ
kaśyapeśaṃ namaskṛtya namaskṛtya harikeśavanaṃ harikeśavanaṃ tataḥ
vaidyanāthaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā dhruveśamatha vīkṣya ca
asthikṣepataḍāge ca dṛṣṭvā vai kīkaseśvaram
bhārabhūtaṃ tato natvā citragupteśvaraṃ tataḥ
citraghaṇṭāṃ praṇamyā'tha tataḥ paśupatīśvaram
pitāmaheśvaraṃ gatvā tatastu kalaśeśvaram
candreśastvatha vīreśo vidyeśo'gnīśa eva ca
nāgeśvarī hariścandraścintāmaṇivināyakaḥ
senāvināyakaścā'tha dravṭavyaḥ sarvavighnahṛt
vasiṣṭhavāmadevau ca mūrtirūpadharāvubhau
draṣṭavyau yatnataḥ kāśyāṃ mahāvighnavināśinau
sīmāvināyakaṃ cā'tha karuṇeśaṃ tato vrajet
trisandhyeśo viśālākṣī dharmeśo viśvabāhukā
āśāvināyakaścā'tha vṛddhādityastataḥ punaḥ
caturvaktreśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ brāhmīśastu tataḥ paraḥ
tato manaḥprakāmeśa īśāneśastataḥ param
caṇḍīcaṇḍeśvarau dṛśyau bhavānīśaṅkarau tataḥ
duṣṭiṃ praṇamya ca tato rājarājeśamarcayet
lāṅgalīśastato'bhyarcyastatastu nakulīśvaraḥ
parānneśamatho natvā paradravyeśvaraṃ tataḥ
pratigraheśvaraṃ vā'pi niṣkalaṅkeśameva ca
gaṅgeśo'bhyarcyastato jñānavāpyāṃ snānaṃ samācaret
nandikeśaṃ tārakeśaṃ mahākāleśvaraṃ tataḥ
daṇḍapāṇiṃ maheśaṃ ca mokṣeśaṃ praṇamettataḥ
vīrabhadreśvaraṃ natvā avimukteśvaraṃ tataḥ
vināyakāṃstataḥ pañca viśvanāthaṃ tato vrajet
antargṛhasya yātreyaṃ yathāvad yā mayā kṛtā
nyūnātiriktayā śambhuḥ prīyatāmanayā vibhuḥ
iti mantraṃ samuccārya kṣaṇaṃ vai muktimaṇḍape
viśramya yāyād bhavanaṃ niṣpāpaḥ puṇyavānnaraḥ
samprāpya vāsaraṃ viṣṇorviṣṇutīrtheṣu sarvataḥ
kāryā yātrā prayatnena mahāpuṇyasamṛddhaye
duḥkhaṃ rudrapiśācatvaṃ na bhavedyasya pūjanāt
śraddhāpūrvamimā yātrāḥ kartavyāḥ kṣetravāsibhiḥ
parvasvapi viśeṣeṇa kāryā yātrāśca sarvataḥ
na vandhyaṃ divasaṃ kuryādvinā yātrāṃ kvacitkṛtī
yasya vandhyaṃ dinaṃ yātaṃ kāśyāṃ nivasataḥ sataḥ
sa daṣṭaḥ kālasarpeṇa sa dṛṣṭo mṛtyunā sphuṭam
sa muṣṭastatra divase viśveśo yatra nekṣitaḥ
maṇikartyāṃ tu yaḥ snāto yo viśveśaṃ niraikṣata
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
dṛśyo viśveśvaro nityaṃ snātavyā maṇikarṇikā
vyāsa uvāca
sūta skāndamidaṃ śrutvā kāśīmāhātmyamuttamam
snātvā sarvāṇi tīrthāni yacchreyaḥ samupārjyate
kāśīkhaṇḍasya śravaṇāttatsyāt sūta na saṃśayaḥ
datvā dānāni sarvāṇi kṛtvā yajñānanekaśaḥ
śravaṇādasya khaṇḍasya labhate tanna saṃśayaḥ
adhītya caturo vedān sāṅgān yatphalamāpyate
kāśīkhaṇḍaṃ samākarṇya tatphalaṃ labhyate naraiḥ
gayāyāṃ śrāddhadānācca yathā tṛpyanti pūrvajāḥ
tathaitacchravaṇānnṛṇāṃ tṛpnuvanti pitāmahāḥ
taiśca sarvapurāṇāni śrutāni sthirabuddhibhiḥ
kāśīkhaṇḍaṃ śrutaṃ yaiśca sarveṣāṃ śreyasāṃ padam
śrutāśva sarvadharmāstairmahāpuṇyaikarāśibhiḥ
śrutaṃ yaiḥ sthiracetobhiḥ kāśīmāhātmyamuttamam
japettatkhaṇḍamakhilaṃ śrotavyaṃ śraddhayā dvijāḥ
śṛṇuyādekamapi ya ākhyānaṃ kāśikhaṇḍajam
śrutāni tena sarvāṇi dharmaśāstrāṇyasaṃśayam
kāraṇaṃ sarvakāmāpteḥ kāśīkhaṇḍamidaṃ smṛtam
etacchravaṇataḥ puṃsāṃ kaivalyaṃ naiva dūrataḥ
prīṇantyamartyāḥ sarve'pi brahmaviṣṇuśivādayaḥ
hṛṣṭaḥ sarvo bhavedeva bhūtagrāmaścaturvidhaḥ
mahimaśravaṇādasmādvārāṇasyā na saṃśayaḥ
pādamātraṃ tadardhaṃ vā tvekaṃ vyākhyānamuttamam
tasmiṃstuṣṭe hi santuṣṭo viśveśo nā'tra saṃśayaḥ
yatraitatpaṭhyate khaṇḍaṃ parānandasamāśrayam
ya idaṃ śṛṇuyādvidvān yaścedaṃ śrāvayet sudhīḥ
yaḥ paṭhedapi puṇyātmā te sarve rudramūrtayaḥ
akhilāni purāṇāni tena dattāni nā'nyathā
atrā''khyānāni yāvanti ślokā yāvanta eva hi
tathā padāni yāvanti varṇā yāvanta eva hi
yāvantyapi ca mātrāṇi yāvatyaḥ padapaṅktayaḥ
guṇe sūtrāṇi yāvanti yāvantaḥ paṭatantavaḥ
tāvadyugasahastrāṇi dātā svarge mahīyate
etaddvādaśakṛtvo yaḥ śṛṇuyāt khaṇḍamuttamam
aputraḥ śṛṇuyādyastu susnātaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ
yo yastaṃ taṃ sa sa sadā śrutyaitat prāpnuyāt kṛtī
śṛṇuyāddūradeśe'pi yaḥ kāśīkhaṇḍamuttamam
sa kāśīvāsapuṇyasya bhājanaṃ syācchivājñayā
saubhāgyaṃ cā'pi sarvatra prāpnuyānnirmalāśayaḥ
sarveṣāṃ maṅgalānāṃ ca mahāmaṅgalamuttamam
iti śrīskandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe anukramaṇikānāma śatatamo'dhyāyaḥ
samāptaṃ cedaṃ kāśīkhaṇḍam
bhaktecchopāttadehāya kṛṣṇāya haraye namaḥ
nyāye kāṇādavartmanyatha ca gurutaro gautamo vā'kṣapādaḥ
sāṃkhye yo devahūtyātmaja iva hi tathā vāsukiryogaśāstre
prākkāṇḍe bhaṭṭatulyaḥ sa jayati paramaḥ śrīsurendro gururnaḥ
vedānte'tha purāṇabhāratavidhau śrīsatyavatyātmajaḥ
sāṃkhye śrīkapilaḥ kaṇāda iha yo vaiśeṣike gautamaḥ
bhaṭṭācāryacaturbhujo vijayate prākkāṇḍakaumārilaḥ
sakośā ca vikośā ca dve ṭīke likhite mayā
yatra yasyā'bhilāṣaḥ syāt sā tena parigṛhyatām
āsītkaśyapavaṃśabhūṣaṇaṃmaṇirmānyo mukundapriyo
steneyaṃ vihitā hitāya viduṣāṃ ṭīkā budhairvīkṣyatām
kāśyāṃ śrīpuruṣottamena viduṣā bhaṭṭena śuddhātmanā
tantrādhyātmapurāṇabhāratavidopāsyopakaṃsāriṇā
rāmānandamunīndravaryakṛtayā gūḍhārthayā ṭīkayā
samyak saṅkalitaṃ hitāya viduṣāṃ śrīkāśikhaṇḍaṃ mahat
iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācārya bhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣya śrīrāmendravanaśiṣyeṇa caitanya
vanā'paraparyāyeṇa rāmānandena kṛtāyāṃ kāśīkhaṇḍaṭīkāyāṃ śatatamo'dhyāyaḥ
samāptā ceyaṃ kāśīkhaṇḍaṭīkā
dohā kāśīkhaṃḍa punīta yaha karata sumaṃgala vṛddhi
sanpūrṇānanda saṃskṛta viśvavi
